Coach Floral Eau The Parfum was created by Shyamala Maisondieu, Nadege le Garlantezec and Natalie Gracia-Cetto. Top notes are Pineapple, Pink Pepper, Orange, Bergamot and Lemon; middle notes are Gardenia, Tea Rose, Jasmine Sambac and Hedione; base notes are Musk, Patchouli, Woody Notes, Vanilla and Sandalwood. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>"Coach Floral Eau de Parfum is inspired by Coach's signature leather tea roses. The feminine scent opens with a splash of citrus coeur and a touch of effervescent pink peppercorn with radiant pineapple sorbet. The heart reveals a bouquet of fragrant flowers-rose tea, jasmine sambac and gardenia-before an enveloping dry-down to elegant creamy wood, patchouli essence and musky notes".</p>

In the vein of Chance eau Tendre--youthful and sweet. Average projection and decent longevity.<br />
<br />
Edit: I have continued to wear it, hoping to fall in love with it, and it's just not happening. However I wanted to mention that I do get pineapple after 5-6 hours. It's not in the top notes as the pyramid would indicate. Smells very much like Dole pineapple juice. <br />
Feeling: Makes me feel like I just walked our from getting my hair professionally done. Blow out and all. I bought this because of the hedione. I love that note in fragrances-- I feel like it saves the whole note pyramid from being too "designer" <br />

<br />

Husband is pleased with it. I really enjoy it especially since I usually hate gardenia in fragrances but this gardenia is creamy. the white florals in here are not heady- they're milky.<br />
<br />
Really pleasant. I hiked with my baby in tow throughout the mall to test at Macy's and ended up purchasing the 50ml at ross.<br />
<br />
50 ml at Macy's is $90 something<br />
The 100ml is I think $115 <br />
<br />

It's in the realm of all the blush pink perfumes, smells very feminine, soft, floral-fruity. Not completely generic though. There is some fun sweetness and white floral milkiness to it, which makes me instantly think of Barbie. A Barbie perfume. Young, joyful, pretty and naive. It gets a bit more interesting nuances in the dry-down.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="2065609"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=2065609#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2038870" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The vanilla notes strengthen through time, makes the perfume sweeter and sweeter. The woody notes is hardly noticeable, but it’s a good point because I don’t like woody notes. <br />
Lovely for a university student. Not too juvenile. An easy to grab perfume in spring. The bottle is cute. <br />
Moderate sillage, moderate lasting power.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="1804717"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=1804717#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1772846" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1300504">rachelsedge</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-05-06">05/06/21 13:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I am not sure why my body chemistry works so differently with this perfume than others on here. The opening does not smell fruity at all to me - I only get a blast of the pink pepper and gardenia. I don't detect much warmth (no vanilla, sandalwood, etc) in the drydown. either. As the review below me puts it, it smells like a "jumble" of florals. On me, it is also SPICY. No clue why I pull so much spice. I knew there was pink pepper in this, and I don't normally mind that, but it doesn't go away on me so it's just a bizarre spicy floral.<br />
<br />
I wouldn't say it smells bad, necessarily. It definitely smells like "Coach". My husband said I smelled good. It just wasn't at all what I was expecting based on the name and the notes. I may try my sample a few more times, but will not be purchasing the full size.<br />
<br />
ETA: Couldn't stand the scent on me... Regifted even the sample!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="1338745"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=1338745#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1337774" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It is fresh but still sweet, uncomplicated fruity floral that lasts all day on me. My fave stage it is in the dry down, approx 1.5 hours when the tartness comes through.<br />
Projection is ok, comfortable. I feel self-conscious with a beast projection so this suits me. Maybe it is not groundbreaking but I like having it in my collection as an easy reach, feminine, pleasant scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="1266481"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=1266481#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1266412" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Lovely fruity opening of light fresh pineapple, followed by soft floral and peppery notes. The citrus notes give it a clean and extra fresh spin.<br />
<br />
This would be perfect for everyday daytime wear all throughout spring to summer. It's a bit generic, yes, but it's also something that will lift your mood instantly, which is why it's been my travel perfume over the last year. Perfect pick me up on or after long flights and great easy pick when you're just out and about to explore a new place.<br />
<br />
Sillage is moderate, but can be upped with amount of sprays. Longevity on me is surprisingly good. In European weather it sticks to my skin the entire day, in India more like half a day.<br />
<br />
If fruity-fresh and uncomplicated is your thing, do give it a sniff. Safe blind buy material, I'd say. I cannot imagine anyone being completely put off by this. And if it's not 100% you're thing you'll definitely find someone around you who'll happily take it off your hands.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="1195146"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=1195146#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1191078" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

You made a fruity floral done right!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="1164901"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=1164901#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1150197" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1227754">spicyramen</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-02-28">02/28/20 07:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance opens on a lovely, bright pineapple note then dries down more floral and only the slightest bit powdery. Definitely way less sweet than the Floral Blush version (which I enjoy more by the way) but this is nice too. Not everyone can take sweet fragrances so Coach Floral is much more friendly. I also found this fragrance to be more complex than the Floral Blush version so for those wanting something that isn't linear, this one is good to try. The longevity is average on me and stays close to the skin after a few hours. <br />
<br />
Another thing to note is that although Floral Blush is a flanker version of Coach the Fragrance, it smells very different to the original (this can be said with the other flankers too so it can be justified if you wanted to buy each version of the perfume). I feel Floral blush is like the younger sister of the original. <br />
<br />
I will say that I think the bottle of this is so pretty with it's flower tag and rose gold hardware. It makes it stand out compared to the other versions!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="1150197"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=1150197#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1148241" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc985356" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Callisa&#039;sBlueSky"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/960584"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.960584.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Callisa&#039;sBlueSky" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chloe/Chloe-Eau-de-Parfum-1733.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.1733.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Chloé Eau de Parfum"title="Chloé Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma985356ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd985356" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/960584">Callisa&#039;sBlueSky</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-09-25">09/25/18 21:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Coach Floral seemed nice and I love rose so I decided to give this a try. The opening is a strong sweet pineapple which I love. But after a few minutes this fragrance becomes so sugary sweet and creamy. I don't dislike sweet scents but I was expecting a floral perfume not a sweet gourmet scent. I have no idea if it is only my skin chemistry amplifying the creamy sweetness. Sadly I get no rose from this.  <br />
<br />
About an hour later the sweetness finally settles and I get some creamy gardenia and a tiny whiff of fresh jasmine. Floral finally becomes a floral perfume on me an hour after application. Unfortunately still no rose. At this point it smells so familiar I swear I have or had a perfume that smells almost identical to this I just cannot put my finger on it. But it is familiar in a nice way, I received many compliments on this fragrance. I was told I smell “classy” and “feminine” and “girly but fresh” by people.<br />
<br />
This is overall a lovely spring scent and seems to behave quite well in moderate heat. Silage is about an arm’s length which is how I prefer my perfumes and the longevity is amazing it lasted over 12 hours on me. Floral is not bad it is a nice, safe scent and should be well received by the majority of people. But to me Floral is a bit too generic, a bit too safe. Girly, sweet and creamy which settles into a more white floral sheer scent. Ideal for daytime in spring or early summer.<br />
<br />
EDIT: I aquired another pretty generous sample of this and was wearing it on and off for a few days. I came to really appreciate the clean soapiness of this. I still don't get much straight up rose, it is more like a lightly scented rose soap to me with a fresh, almost aquatic feel in the background. It is really nice and refreshing in this intense summer heat we currently have. If I find this at a good deal I will get a full bottle. The longevity of this perfume is insane on my skin, it lasts through baths or showers. That has never happened before even with my Chanel and Dior perfumes. Coach Floral is the perfume version of waterproof, everything-proof mascara that resists all forms of cleansers.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="985356"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=985356#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent983867" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I would even say aromatic or balsamic. Mostly it's jasmine and rose. Some pineapple balances out this floral. Bit plastic-y feel from pepper note. Patchouli is present, but not too strong.<br />
<br />
Would fit young and feminine woman. I feel this can be all year around perfume. Little bit tropical, sweet but not too sweet for summer. Aromatic, slightly warm and cozy for colder seasons.<br />
<br />
After about hour most of sweetness and floral notes are gone. It became mostly softly aromatic and peppery. I wouldn't say it's synthetic, at least not in bad way, but also it's not natural scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="961522"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=961522#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent959042" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1109580">Lilacs&amp;Lavender</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-07-05">07/05/18 23:36</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It is mid-Winter where I live and I am wearing this today as a pick me up. This is delightful, fun and fresh. Coach Floral isn't a sugary sweet scent, but more like a long cool drink of Tonic infused with pieces of fresh fruit. It is close to the original but distinct enough to stand on its own. Although the notes are completely different, I think if you enjoy Chanel Chance Eau Tendre you will like this too.<br />
<br />
The silage and longevity are moderate, however if you intend to wear this to the office, I wouldn't recommend more than a couple of sprays. I suspect that the fruity sweetness might annoy others if it was over sprayed.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="959042"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=959042#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent958677" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1146205">dansey4</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-06-13">06/13/18 04:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Love the pineapple and citrus blends. I love it but I would prefer wearing it in summer rather than in winter. It is too sweet to wear it in winter time.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="952000"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=952000#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent949193" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc949193" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Justapixel"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1060887"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1060887.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Justapixel" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma949193ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd949193" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1060887">Justapixel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-06-03">06/03/18 18:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I was in the Coach store, having a luggage tag hot-stamped. On the way out, I saw the perfume tray and ignoring the paper, I put a spray directly on my arm. I cannot pass by a perfume tray, can you?  <br />
<br />
The first notes are definitely a sweet, spicy pineapple and while pretty, I was not instantly smitten. I also wasn’t paying much attention, having to navigate a very crowded mall. I didn’t get to sniff and analyze and take it in like I normally would. <br />
<br />
By the time I got to the car though, I was very impressed.The one small spray filled my senses and the car and all the way home I enjoyed the deeply feminine and yet spicy peppercorn scent.  I found it quite lovely, and of course, it struck me as something I should have in my collection. <br />
<br />
It’s been hours now and that one spritz is still going strong. My husband noticed how good I smelled and sitting here, I still get wafts of the fragrance. It’s long lasting, certainly. It is, however, a very hot day and my air-conditioning is broken. <br />
<br />
So in my opinion, Rose is the dominant scent, but it is not a fresh, natural  real rose like in Paul Smith’s fragrance, or as in Joe Malone’s Red Roses. It’s a bit bit dirty, a bit purple, more along the lines of Stella or Chloe’s Roses de Chloe. The peppercorn is masterfully done, it enhances the flowers and toned down the girliness. Patchouli is coming forth, but musk and woods is gentle. <br />
<br />
It’s a very pretty perfume. Oddly enough, I have not had or remember smelling any fragrances in the Coach line so I don’t know how it holds up compared to others. I do know that I like this one very much, and the next time I need a Rose perfume, it will be at the top of my list.<br />
<br />
Edit: Less than a week later I had to have it. It is now the scent I use most often. I adore it and spray it liberally-when I won’t be sitting too close to people, that is. Silage and longevity are very good on me but I suspect this fragrance with it’s peppery tones might bring coughs to the perfume sensitive. Oh, and the Rose is not as obvious as I had thought-of course it is there, but I would not classify this with my rose scents.  It is the peppercorn is the star of this spicy show, with the later patchouli. . <br />
<br />
It may be ok for an office if you aren’t trapped in a cube with others. Coach has improved their handbags and perhaps this fragrance is part of upscaling the line. It stands well on its own and I’m quite pleased with my purchase.it fits in with youth or a stylish mature woman.  This scent also brings me cheer so I overdo when I have lost my smile. I do get compliments from stylists, aestheticians, as others but not yet from somebody on the street. It’s a very well done fragrance and amI  very happy to have bought it. <br />
<br />
Oddly, I don’t want to get Coach’s previous versions. I usually enjoy seeing how a perfumer goes from first to flanker, what’s changed, what’s highlighted. With Coach Floral though, I think I will let this stand alone. For me it’s close to perfection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="949193"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=949193#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent937786" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/6977">DarlingNikki</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-03-01">03/01/18 19:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The initial blast of pineapple is quite lovely, but as this begins to settle down I'm smelling something off-putting.  Smells like those little Valentine's Day candy hearts with the sayings and I think it might the way the pink pepper is mixing in with the white florals.  There's a weird nearly cough inducing sweetness in this that I'm not liking, but I'll give it more time and see if it grows on me.  Initial impression is not good...<br />
<br />
Update: okay, tried this again and the impression is still not favorable.  I want to like this and right out of the gate I do, but within seconds as it starts to dry down the citruses mix with the jasmine and produce a very off-putting bad breath/sharp undertone that I can't take.  The pineapple, gardenia and pink pepper are quite nice in the opening, but that jasmine/citrus combo kills this one for me.<br />
<br />
EDIT: Bought this one by mistake at Ulta looking for the newest flanker called Floral Blush and now that I've spent more time with it, honestly, it's not that bad.  It smells kind of shampoo-ish to me, quite simple and not nearly as sweet as most people are getting, at least not on paper.  I've yet to try it on skin for a proper wearing--think I will as the temperatures are hitting triple digits.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="917280"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=917280#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent913525" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="1276214"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=1276214#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent949193" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc949193" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Justapixel"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1060887"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1060887.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Justapixel" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma949193ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd949193" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1060887">Justapixel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-06-03">06/03/18 18:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I was in the Coach store, having a luggage tag hot-stamped. On the way out, I saw the perfume tray and ignoring the paper, I put a spray directly on my arm. I cannot pass by a perfume tray, can you?  <br />
<br />
The first notes are definitely a sweet, spicy pineapple and while pretty, I was not instantly smitten. I also wasn’t paying much attention, having to navigate a very crowded mall. I didn’t get to sniff and analyze and take it in like I normally would. <br />
<br />
By the time I got to the car though, I was very impressed.The one small spray filled my senses and the car and all the way home I enjoyed the deeply feminine and yet spicy peppercorn scent.  I found it quite lovely, and of course, it struck me as something I should have in my collection. <br />
<br />
It’s been hours now and that one spritz is still going strong. My husband noticed how good I smelled and sitting here, I still get wafts of the fragrance. It’s long lasting, certainly. It is, however, a very hot day and my air-conditioning is broken. <br />
<br />
So in my opinion, Rose is the dominant scent, but it is not a fresh, natural  real rose like in Paul Smith’s fragrance, or as in Joe Malone’s Red Roses. It’s a bit bit dirty, a bit purple, more along the lines of Stella or Chloe’s Roses de Chloe. The peppercorn is masterfully done, it enhances the flowers and toned down the girliness. Patchouli is coming forth, but musk and woods is gentle. <br />
<br />
It’s a very pretty perfume. Oddly enough, I have not had or remember smelling any fragrances in the Coach line so I don’t know how it holds up compared to others. I do know that I like this one very much, and the next time I need a Rose perfume, it will be at the top of my list.<br />
<br />
Edit: Less than a week later I had to have it. It is now the scent I use most often. I adore it and spray it liberally-when I won’t be sitting too close to people, that is. Silage and longevity are very good on me but I suspect this fragrance with it’s peppery tones might bring coughs to the perfume sensitive. Oh, and the Rose is not as obvious as I had thought-of course it is there, but I would not classify this with my rose scents.  It is the peppercorn is the star of this spicy show, with the later patchouli. . <br />
<br />
It may be ok for an office if you aren’t trapped in a cube with others. Coach has improved their handbags and perhaps this fragrance is part of upscaling the line. It stands well on its own and I’m quite pleased with my purchase.it fits in with youth or a stylish mature woman.  This scent also brings me cheer so I overdo when I have lost my smile. I do get compliments from stylists, aestheticians, as others but not yet from somebody on the street. It’s a very well done fragrance and amI  very happy to have bought it. <br />
<br />
Oddly, I don’t want to get Coach’s previous versions. I usually enjoy seeing how a perfumer goes from first to flanker, what’s changed, what’s highlighted. With Coach Floral though, I think I will let this stand alone. For me it’s close to perfection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="949193"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=949193#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1289212" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1133260">latafan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-07-02">07/02/20 07:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I can't believe I almost went through a bottle of this and didn't write anything about it yet.<br />
<br />
Lovely fruity opening of light fresh pineapple, followed by soft floral and peppery notes. The citrus notes give it a clean and extra fresh spin.<br />
<br />
This would be perfect for everyday daytime wear all throughout spring to summer. It's a bit generic, yes, but it's also something that will lift your mood instantly, which is why it's been my travel perfume over the last year. Perfect pick me up on or after long flights and great easy pick when you're just out and about to explore a new place.<br />
<br />
Sillage is moderate, but can be upped with amount of sprays. Longevity on me is surprisingly good. In European weather it sticks to my skin the entire day, in India more like half a day.<br />
<br />
If fruity-fresh and uncomplicated is your thing, do give it a sniff. Safe blind buy material, I'd say. I cannot imagine anyone being completely put off by this. And if it's not 100% you're thing you'll definitely find someone around you who'll happily take it off your hands.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="48115"comment_id="1195146"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html?ccid=1195146#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent937786" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
I bought a travel size and gave it several tested days before returning it:<br />
It’s fine. It’s just…fine. It smells nice and pretty…but I like a little more sex appeal in my perfume. It’s a little too clean for my liking, and it smells more like a really nice soap than a perfume. There’s just no musk on me. No Bueno!<br />
The longevity was poor and the sillage wasn't great.<br />
<br />
I smell like someone that doesn’t want to offend anyone, which is a bit too boring for my taste ;)<br />
<br />
Feminine for all ages (it's coach, after all) this would be perfect for those that like a light clean professional feminine scent to wear at work in the summer. There's nothing significant in any of these perfumes. The blend of each individual perfume smells almost the same as one another. There's no uniqueness in Coach perfumes. Although some Juicy Couture perfumes do stand out but still weak and subtle. None of these brands project well. You smell like a mix of fruity floral but there's no character to it. There's no depth. You just smell like you sprayed on perfume and that's about it. Don't waste your money on these brands, you can buy way cheaper perfumes with excellent character, projection and longevity.
